<section>
<section.front>
<outline.name.block>
<label>&sect;</label>
<designator>10:1</designator>
<name>Scope</name>
</outline.name.block>
</section.front>
<section.body>
►<para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|1|10:1">
<para.text>
This chapter contains forms for final judgments, some forms of orders that are final and some forms of orders that are not final, but partake more of judgments than of the usual interlocutory orders. This chapter also includes forms for final process and for enforcing final judgments.
</para.text>
</para>
</section.body>
</section>
<section>
<section.front>
<outline.name.block>
<label>&sect;</label>
<designator>10:2</designator>
<name>Form and procedure</name>
</outline.name.block>
</section.front>
<section.body>
►<para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|2|10:2">
<para.text>
Judgments and final orders, as well as the orders in this chapter that are not final, contain a caption in the form of the action, a designation as the appropriate judgment or order, a commencement that sometimes includes findings of fact and a body that contains the adjudications made by the judgment or order. See ►<x>&sect;2:2; ►st.ref.id="I03XWRW">Fla. R. Civ. P. 1.100(c); ►<field>st.ref.id="I015V9P"</field>Fla. Fam. L. R. P. 12.100(c). Judgments and orders are completed by a conclusion that gives the date and place of entry and the signature of the judge. A notation of the parties or attorneys to whom conformed copies of the judgment have been sent is in the lower left-hand part of the form.
</x>
</para.text>
</para>
►<para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|2|10:2">
<para.text>
After a judgment is entered, it must be filed with the clerk, and recorded. If it is not a final judgment or order, it may be recorded if the court so orders. Interlocutory orders that deal with the title to or possession of real property should always be recorded.
</para.text>
</para>
►<para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|2|10:2">
<para.text>
The commencement of final judgments differs. There is one form for an application for judgment after default, others for judgment after motion for judgment on the pleadings, for summary judgment, for dismissal and for jury trials and nonjury trials. The commencement should recite the predicate for its entry, such as one of the motions, a jury or nonjury trial, and then move on to the adjudicatory paragraphs. Most lawyers call the judgment after a motion for summary judgment a summary judgment. It is not. It is a final judgment granted after a motion for summary judgment. It can properly be called a summary final judgment, but it is better to call it simply a final judgment.
</para.text>
</para>
►<para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|2|10:2">
<para.text>
The commencement must contain findings of fact in some cases.<trace> </trace><trace>►</trace><trace>The failure to include the required findings of fact in </trace><trace>a</trace><trace> final judgment</trace><trace> leave the judgment open to attack by rehearing, appeal, and ultimately a new trial</trace><trace>. </trace><trace>►</trace><trace>See Fla. R. Civ. P. 1.530</trace><trace> and Fam. L. R. P. 12.530.</trace>
</para.text>
</para>
►<para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|2|10:2">
<para.text>
►st.ref.id="I02T6UB">Rule 1.560(c) of the Florida Rules of Civil Procedure was amended to authorize a requirement that a judgment debtor furnish a fact information sheet to the judgment creditor's attorney. See ►<field>st.ref.id="I05VWWO"</field>Fla. R. Civ. P. Form 1.977. The form may be subject to challenge in requiring a nonparty spouse to divulge separate property. A similar requirement form is authorized for small claims. See ►<field>st.ref.id="I052Z2G"</field>Fla. Sm. Cl. R. 7.221. The provision for the requirement is in ►<x>&sect;10:13. It can be added to any other form to which it is applicable.
</x>
</para.text>
</para>
►<para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|2|10:2">
<para.text>
Costs are included in all of the forms of final judgments. Many times court costs cannot be awarded when judgment is entered so a motion to tax costs must be filed and a separate order taxing costs entered. See ►<x>&sect;7:<trace>200</trace><trace.deleted/>&sect;<trace.deleted/>; ►<x>&sect;7:201; ►<x>&sect;7:30<trace>5</trace><trace.deleted/>.
</x>
</para.text>
</para>
►<para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|2|10:2">
<para.text>
For a money judgment to become a lien on the judgment debtor's property it must contain the prevailing party's address and the non-prevailing party's address and Social Security number if known or an affidavit must be recorded with the information at the same time as the certified copy of the judgment.
</para.text>
</para>
<item.reference.block>
<item.reference>
<name.block>
<label>Author's</label>
<designator>&lsqb;'Comment'&rsqb;</designator>
</name.block></item.reference></item.reference.block>
►<para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|2|10:2">
<para.text>
See ►st.ref.id="I02T71J">&sect;28.222(3)(c), Fla. Stat.; ►<field>st.ref.id="I02T776"</field>&sect;28.29, Fla. Stat. See ►<field>cc.ref.id="I05QEGP"</field>Sun Bank/Southwest, N.A. v. Schad, 482 So. 2d 554 (Fla. 2d DCA 1986) for the immediate issuance of the execution; and ►<field>cc.ref.id="I05NLHH"</field>Robinson v. Sterling Door &amp; Window Co., Inc., 698 So. 2d 570 (Fla. 1st DCA 1997) for the requirement of the parties' addresses and the judgment debtor's party's Social Security number for money judgments. See ►<field>st.ref.id="I05VWI9"</field>&sect;55.10(2), Fla. Stat.
</para.text>
</para>
</section.body>
</section>

</form.text>

<form.unit>

<form.text>

</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|3|10:3">
<form.text>

</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|3|10:3">
<form.text>
Defendant shall account to plaintiff for plaintiff's share of the net proceeds of the sale of the remaining assets of the joint venture:
</form.text>
</form.para>

<form.text>
p.fl="none">within ten days after the sale of each asset.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|3|10:3">
<form.text>
Plaintiff &lsqb;NAME OF PLAINTIFF&rsqb;, whose address is &lsqb;address of plaintiff&rsqb;, recover from defendant &lsqb;NAME OF DEFENDANT&rsqb; &lsqb;OPTIONAL:, whose address is &lsqb;address of defendant&rsqb; and the last four digits of Social Security number are &lsqb;last four numbers of Social Security number&rsqb;,&rsqb; the sum of $&lsqb;dollar amount of judgment&rsqb; with interest of $&lsqb;dollar amount of interests&rsqb; to the date of this judgment, and costs in the sum of $&lsqb;dollar amount of costs&rsqb;, making a total of $&lsqb;total dollar amount of costs&rsqb;, with interest at the rate prescribed by law, for which let execution issue forthwith.
</form.text>

<para.text>

This form assumes the attorney fee disallowance is for an improper charge and the balance of the accounting is proper. If the accounting shows no debt due plaintiff, paragraph 4 would be changed to the usual judgment for defendant. See ►<x>&sect;10:12. This form can be used in family actions: See ►<x>&sect;5:5, Comment.
</x>
</para.text>

►<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|5|10:5">
<form.text>
This action was heard on defendant's motion for rehearing and
</form.text>
</form.para>
►<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|5|10:5">
<form.text>
IT IS ADJUDGED that:
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|5|10:5">
<form.text>
The final judgment dated &lsqb;date of judgment&rsqb; entered in this action and recorded in Official Records Book &lsqb;number of record&rsqb; at page &lsqb;number of page&rsqb; of the public records of &lsqb;name of county&rsqb;, Florida is vacated.

<item.reference.block>
<item.reference>
<name.block>
<label>Author's</label>
<designator>&lsqb;'Comment'&rsqb;</designator>
</name.block></item.reference></item.reference.block>
►<para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|7|10:7">
<para.text>
This form was derived from ►cc.ref.id="I02Z37H">Musselwhite v. Oleson, 53 So. 944 (Fla. 1910). Rescission and cancellation are similar, but distinguishable because rescission effects a judicial voiding of the instrument. Cancellation requires the physical surrender of the instrument in order to effect the voiding. See ►<field>cc.ref.id="I02Z38M"</field>Willis v. Fowler, 136 So. 358 (Fla. 1931). Thus a recorded instrument can be rescinded, but it cannot be canceled since it is a part of the public records.
</para.text>
</para>
</section.body>

►<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|8|10:8">
<form.text>
This action seeks a writ of certiorari to the City of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of city&rsqb;</inline.instr> to rezone the property described in the petition to permit construction of a commercial establishment. The property is presently zoned for single family residences only. The City refused to rezone the property at a public hearing. Petitioner contends that the City refused the rezoning petition because of the political pressure brought by the number of opponents of the rezoning request who were present at the public hearing. Petitioner did not have a court reporter present and the record from the electronic recording machines is so poor that the events transpiring at the hearing cannot be determined with certainty. Since there is an inadequate record of the proceedings below from which it can be determined that the City erred as a matter of law.
</form.text>
</form.para>
►<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|8|10:8">
<form.text>
IT IS ADJUDGED that:
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|8|10:8">
<form.text>
Certiorari is denied.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|8|10:8">
<form.text>
The court reserves jurisdiction to tax costs.
</form.text>
</form.para>

ORDERED at &lsqb;name of city&rsqb;, Florida on &lsqb;date of order&rsqb;.
</form.text>

        <row><entry><field>entry.resize="same"</field></entry><entry><field>entry.resize="same"</field>Petitioner,</entry><entry><field>entry.resize="same"</field></entry></row>
        <row><entry><field>entry.resize="same"</field>v.</entry><entry><field>entry.resize="same"</field>CASE &lsqb;CASE NUMBER&rsqb;</entry></row>
        <row><entry><field>entry.resize="same"</field>&lsqb;NAME OF RESPONDENT&rsqb;,</entry><entry><field>entry.resize="same"</field></entry></row>

►<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|9|10:9">
<form.text>
This action seeks a writ of certiorari to the County Court of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of county&rsqb;</inline.instr>, Florida, to review a discovery order. Petitioner in this action is plaintiff in the county court and seeks damages for breach of contract. Defendant counterclaimed for malicious interference. Defendant propounded interrogatories seeking information about plaintiff's assets, liabilities, customer names and other financial information. The pleadings do not seek punitive damages at this stage and no discovery has been conducted as contemplated by ►st.ref.id="I05Q5XJ">&sect;768.72 Florida Statutes as a predicate for amending to plead punitive damages.
</form.text>
</form.para>
►<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|9|10:9">
<form.text>
Plaintiff objected to interrogatories <inline.instr>&lsqb;designation of interrogatories&rsqb;</inline.instr> that seek financial and business information on the grounds that customers' names were a trade secret and financial information was not relevant. The county court overruled the objections and ordered plaintiff to provide the requested discovery.
</form.text>
</form.para>
►<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|9|10:9">
<form.text>
Defendant supports the county court order on the grounds that it may lead to admissible evidence and provide the basis for punitive damages. Plaintiff contends that discovery on that basis is premature.
</form.text>
</form.para>
►<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|9|10:9">
<form.text>
The court finds that the interrogatories are premature, except interrogatory 16 seeking customer names, so
</form.text>
</form.para>
►<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|9|10:9">
<form.text>
IT IS ADJUDGED that:
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|9|10:9">
<form.text>
Certiorari is granted and the order of the County Court of &lsqb;name of county&rsqb;, Florida dated &lsqb;date of order&rsqb; overruling plaintiff's objections to defendant's interrogatories is quashed, except for interrogatory &lsqb;designation of interrogatory&rsqb;.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|9|10:9">
<form.text>
This action is remanded to the County Court of &lsqb;name of county&rsqb;, Florida for further proceedings consistent with this judgment.
</form.text>
</form.para>

►<para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|9|10:9">
<para.text>
Note that most certiorari petitions to review discovery orders in the county court will now be submitted the district courts of appeal, not to the circuit court as in the example above. Jurisdiction to issue an extraordinary writ follows appeal jurisdiction, see ►cc.ref.id="I05MOWH">Florida Dept. of Community Affairs v. Escambia County, 582 So. 2d 1237 (Fla. 1st DCA 1991); ►<field>cc.ref.id="I05MOPC"</field>Wovas v. Tousa Homes, Inc., 940 So. 2d 1166 (Fla. 2d DCA 2006), and the appellate jurisdiction of the circuit court has now been restricted to a limited class of cases. See ►<field>st.ref.id="I04ZP60"</field>&sect;26.012(1), Fla. Stat.
</para.text>
</para>

►<para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|14|10:14">
<para.text>
A judgment for declaratory relief must give the requested declaration. See ►cc.ref.id="I04829L">Ennis v. Warm Mineral Springs, Inc., 203 So. 2d 514 (Fla. 2d DCA 1967); ►<field>cc.ref.id="I04594P"</field>Hildebrandt v. Department of Natural Resources, Division of Interior Resources, 313 So. 2d 73 (Fla. 3d DCA 1975). This applies even when the declaration is against the plaintiff. Paragraph 8 of the form is an adjudication of liability. It is not a judgment for money. This form assumes the pleadings did not contain a predicate for the money judgment. The money judgment can be obtained by a motion for supplemental relief.
</para.text>

<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|22|10:22">
<form.text>
This action was tried before the court. On the evidence presented the court finds that the directors of <inline.instr>&lsqb;NAME OF DEFENDANT CORPORATION&rsqb;</inline.instr> are deadlocked in the management of the corporate affairs and the shareholders are unable to break the deadlock. As a result irreparable injury to the corporate defendant's assets is now being suffered and unless the action taken under this final judgment occurs, the assets will be lost to the shareholders. The corporation has complied with ►st.ref.id="I04BHVZ">&sect;607.1431(4), Fla. Stat., however the shareholders have not elected to purchase the plaintiff's shares, therefore
</form.text>
</form.para>
►<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|22|10:22">
<form.text>
IT IS ADJUDGED that:
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|22|10:22">
<form.text>
Defendant &lsqb;NAME OF DEFENDANT CORPORATION&rsqb; is dissolved effective &lsqb;date of dissolution&rsqb;.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|22|10:22">
<form.text>
The directors shall sell all of the assets of the corporation as soon as possible. When sufficient assets are sold so that all creditors can be paid, the directors of the corporation shall pay the debts of the corporation.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|22|10:22">
<form.text>
If there is an excess of funds after the debts of the corporation are paid, the balance after paying the debts of the corporation shall be paid to the stockholders of the corporation pro rata according to the amounts of stock owned by each.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|22|10:22">
<form.text>
The directors of the corporation shall follow the procedures prescribed by &dblsect;607.1406 and 607.1407, Florida Statutes as may be necessary to dispose of all claims against the corporation by its creditors.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|22|10:22">
<form.text>
The court reserves jurisdiction of the corporation to enforce this judgment and to enter any other orders that may be necessary for the complete and proper disposition of the corporation's assets.
</form.text>
</form.para>

►<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|32|10:32">
<form.text>
This action was tried before the court. On the evidence presented the court finds that plaintiff's attorney has reasonably expended <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of hours&rsqb;</inline.instr> hours in representing plaintiff in this action and that $<inline.instr>&lsqb;dollar hourly rate of attorney's fees&rsqb;</inline.instr> is a reasonable hourly rate for the services and that defendant <inline.instr>&lsqb;NAME OF LIENOR&rsqb;</inline.instr> attorney has reasonably expended <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of hours&rsqb;</inline.instr> hours in the representation of defendant in this action and that $<inline.instr>&lsqb;dollar amount of hourly rate of attorney's fees&rsqb;</inline.instr> is a reasonable hourly rate for the services, so
</form.text>
</form.para>
►<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|32|10:32">
<form.text>
IT IS ADJUDGED that:
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|32|10:32">
<form.text>
Plaintiff &lsqb;NAME OF PLAINTIFF&rsqb;, whose address is &lsqb;address of plaintiff&rsqb;, is due $&lsqb;dollar amount of improvements&rsqb; for labor, services and material furnished to improve the real property described in paragraph 2, $&lsqb;dollar amount of interest&rsqb; as interest to the date of this judgment, $&lsqb;dollar amount of attorney's fees&rsqb; for attorney fees with costs of $&lsqb;dollar amount of costs&rsqb;, making a total of $&lsqb;total dollar amount of judgment&rsqb; that shall bear interest at the rate of &lsqb;rate of interest&rsqb;% a year.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|32|10:32">
<form.text>
Plaintiff holds a construction lien for the total sum superior to any claim or interest of defendant &lsqb;NAME OF DEFENDANT OWNER&rsqb; on the following real property in &lsqb;name of county&rsqb;, Florida:
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|32|10:32">
<form.text>
If the total sum with interest at the rate prescribed in paragraph 1 and all costs of this action accruing subsequent to this judgment are not paid, the clerk of this court shall sell the property at public sale on &lsqb;date of sale&rsqb;, between 11:00 a.m. and 2:00 p.m., to the highest bidder for cash, except as prescribed in paragraphs 4 and 5, at the &lsqb;location of sale&rsqb; door of the courthouse in &lsqb;name of county&rsqb; in accordance with ►st.ref.id="I03HNW1">&sect;45.031, Fla. Stat. The clerk of this court shall receive the service charge pursuant to ►<field>st.ref.id="I03HNUW"</field>&sect;45.035, Fla. Stat. in making, recording, and certifying the sale and title that shall be assessed as costs.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|32|10:32">
<form.text>
Plaintiff shall advance all subsequent costs of this action and shall be reimbursed for them by the clerk if plaintiff is not the purchaser of the property at the sale. If plaintiff is the purchaser, the clerk shall credit plaintiff's bid with the prorated amount specified in paragraph 6, not to exceed the total sum due plaintiff, with interest and costs accruing subsequent to this judgment, or such part of it, as is necessary to fully pay the bid.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|32|10:32">
<form.text>
Defendant &lsqb;NAME OF LIENOR&rsqb; holds a construction lien on the property for labor, services and material furnished to improve the real property described in paragraph 2 of equal dignity and priority with that of plaintiff that has been asserted by crossclaim for $&lsqb;dollar amount of crossclaim&rsqb;, with $&lsqb;dollar amount of interest&rsqb; for interest to the date of this judgment, $&lsqb;dollar amount of attorney's fees&rsqb; for attorney fees with costs of $&lsqb;dollar amount of costs&rsqb;, making a total of $&lsqb;total dollar amount of judgment&rsqb; that shall bear interest at the rate of &lsqb;rate of interest&rsqb;% a year. Paragraph 3 also applies to this lien. If defendant &lsqb;NAME OF LIENOR&rsqb; is the purchaser of the property at the sale, the clerk shall credit defendant's bid with the prorated amount specified in paragraph 6, not to exceed the total sum due defendant, or such part of it as is necessary to fully pay the bid.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|32|10:32">
<form.text>
After filing the certificate of title the clerk shall distribute the proceeds of the sale, so far as they are sufficient, by paying: first, all plaintiff's and defendant &lsqb;NAME OF LIENOR&rsqb; costs; second, documentary stamps affixed to the certificate; third, plaintiff's and defendant &lsqb;NAME OF LIENOR&rsqb; attorney fees; fourth, the total sum due to plaintiff and defendant less the items paid plus interest from this date to the date of the sale; and shall retain any remaining amount for subsequent distribution pursuant to ►st.ref.id="I03HNP6">&sect;45.031 Fla. Stat. If the proceeds are insufficient to pay any item, the proceeds shall be prorated between plaintiff and defendant &lsqb;NAME OF LIENOR&rsqb; in proportion to the amounts of their respective claims in each category.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|32|10:32">
<form.text>
IF THIS PROPERTY IS SOLD AT PUBLIC AUCTION, THERE MAY BE ADDITIONAL MONEY FROM THE SALE AFTER PAYMENT OF PERSONS WHO ARE ENTITLED TO BE PAID FROM THE SALE PROCEEDS PURSUANT TO THIS FINAL JUDGMENT.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|32|10:32">
<form.text>
IF YOU ARE A SUBORDINATE LIENHOLDER CLAIMING A RIGHT TO FUNDS REMAINING AFTER THE SALE, IF ANY, YOU MUST FILE A CLAIM WITH THE CLERK NO LATER THAN THE DATE THAT THE CLERK REPORTS THE FUNDS AS UNCLAIMED. IF YOU FAIL TO FILE A TIMELY CLAIM, YOU WILL NOT BE ENTITLED TO ANY REMAINING FUNDS.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|32|10:32">
<form.text>
On filing the certificate of title defendant &lsqb;NAME OF OWNER&rsqb; and all persons claiming under or against defendant since the filing of the notice of lis pendens shall be foreclosed of all estate in or claim to the property and the purchaser at the sale shall be let into possession of the property.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|32|10:32">
<form.text>
Jurisdiction of this action is retained to enter further orders as are proper including, without limitation, writs of possession and deficiency judgments.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|32|10:32">
<form.text>
ORDERED at &lsqb;name of city&rsqb;, Florida on &lsqb;date of order&rsqb;.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|32|10:32">
<form.text>
Jurisdiction of this action is retained to enter further orders as are proper including, without limitation, writs of possession and deficiency judgments.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|32|10:32">
<form.text>
ORDERED at &lsqb;name of city&rsqb;, Florida on &lsqb;date of order&rsqb;.

►<para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|32|10:32">
<para.text>
This form assumes a foreclosure by plaintiff lienor and another lienor joined as a defendant who foreclosed by crossclaim. This form also assumes a trial. This form has the findings on fees required by ►cc.ref.id="I06RPS8">Florida Patient's Compensation Fund v. Rowe, 472 So. 2d 1145 (Fla. 1985), holding modified by Standard Guar. Ins. Co. v. Quanstrom, 555 So. 2d 828 (Fla. 1990). It shows the method of sale for two lienors whose liens are of equal dignity. See ►<field>st.ref.id="I04ABMA"</field>&sect;713.06(2)(b), Fla. Stat.
</para.text>
</para>

►<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|33|10:33">
<form.text>
This action was tried before the court. On the evidence presented
</form.text>
</form.para>
►<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|33|10:33">
<form.text>
IT IS ADJUDGED that:
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|33|10:33">
<form.text>
Plaintiff &lsqb;NAME OF PLAINTIFF&rsqb;, whose address is &lsqb;address of plaintiff&rsqb;, is due $&lsqb;dollar amount of improvements&rsqb; for labor, services and material furnished to improve the real property described in paragraph 2, $&lsqb;dollar amount of interest&rsqb; as interest to the date of this judgment, with costs of $&lsqb;dollar amount of costs&rsqb;, making a total of $&lsqb;total dollar amount of judgment&rsqb; that shall bear interest at the rate of &lsqb;rate of interest&rsqb;% a year.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|33|10:33">
<form.text>
Plaintiff holds an equitable lien for the total sum superior to any claim or interest of defendants &lsqb;NAME OF DEFENDANT OWNER&rsqb; and &lsqb;NAME OF DEFENDANT LENDER&rsqb; on the following real property in &lsqb;name of county&rsqb;, Florida:
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|33|10:33">
<form.text>
If the total sum with interest at the rate prescribed in paragraph 1 and all costs of this action accruing subsequent to this judgment are not paid, the clerk of this court shall sell the property at public sale on &lsqb;date of sale&rsqb;, between 11:00 a.m. and 2:00 p.m., to the highest bidder for cash, except as prescribed in paragraph 4, at the &lsqb;location of sale&rsqb; door of the courthouse in &lsqb;name of county&rsqb; in accordance with ►st.ref.id="I03RVZV">Section 45.031, Florida Statutes. The clerk of this court shall receive the service charge pursuant to ►<field>st.ref.id="I03HNOZ"</field>&sect;45.035, Fla. Stat. in making, recording, and certifying the sale and title that shall be assessed as costs.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|33|10:33">
<form.text>
Plaintiff shall advance all subsequent costs of this action and shall be reimbursed for them by the clerk if plaintiff is not the purchaser of the property at the sale. If plaintiff is the purchaser, the clerk shall credit plaintiff's bid with the total sum with interest and costs accruing subsequent to this judgment, or such part of it, as is necessary to fully pay the bid.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|33|10:33">
<form.text>
After filing the certificate of title the clerk shall distribute the proceeds of the sale, as far as they are sufficient, by paying: first, plaintiff's costs; second, documentary stamps affixed to the certificate; third, plaintiff's attorney fees; fourth, the total sum due plaintiff, less the items paid, plus interest from this date to the date of the sale; and shall retain any remaining amount for subsequent distribution pursuant to ►st.ref.id="I03HNNR">&sect;45.031 Fla. Stat.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|33|10:33">
<form.text>
IF THIS PROPERTY IS SOLD AT PUBLIC AUCTION, THERE MAY BE ADDITIONAL MONEY FROM THE SALE AFTER PAYMENT OF PERSONS WHO ARE ENTITLED TO BE PAID FROM THE SALE PROCEEDS PURSUANT TO THIS FINAL JUDGMENT.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|33|10:33">
<form.text>
IF YOU ARE A SUBORDINATE LIENHOLDER CLAIMING A RIGHT TO FUNDS REMAINING AFTER THE SALE, IF ANY, YOU MUST FILE A CLAIM WITH THE CLERK NO LATER THAN THE DATE THAT THE CLERK REPORTS THE FUNDS AS UNCLAIMED. IF YOU FAIL TO FILE A TIMELY CLAIM, YOU WILL NOT BE ENTITLED TO ANY REMAINING FUNDS.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|33|10:33">
<form.text>
On filing the certificate of title defendants and all persons claiming under or against defendants since the filing of the notice of lis pendens shall be foreclosed of all estate in or claim to the property and the purchaser at the sale shall be let into possession of the property.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|33|10:33">

Jurisdiction of this action is retained to enter further orders as are proper including, without limitation, writs of possession.

This example was derived from ►cc.ref.id="I06ZD3E">Rabinowitz v. Keefer, 132 So. 297 (Fla. 1931) omitting the findings and incorporating the reason for the action in paragraph 2. Rescission and cancellation are similar, but distinguishable because rescission effects a judicial voiding of the instrument. Cancellation requires the physical surrender of the instrument in order to effect the voiding of it. See ►<field>cc.ref.id="I0308IW"</field>Willis v. Fowler, 136 So. 358 (Fla. 1931).
</para.text>

►<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|63|10:63">
<form.text>
This action was tried before the court on all issues, except compensation for the way of necessity. The court finds that plaintiff is entitled to a statutory way of necessity because plaintiff's property, described hereinafter, is outside any municipality, is used for agricultural purposes and has no practicable route of egress or ingress to the nearest practicable public or private road. Pursuant to the verdict rendered in this action on compensation, the court hereinafter adjudicates the amount of compensation for the way of necessity. On the evidence presented
</form.text>
</form.para>
►<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|63|10:63">
<form.text>
IT IS ADJUDGED that:
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|63|10:63">
<form.text>
Plaintiff &lsqb;NAME OF PLAINTIFF&rsqb; is entitled to a statutory way of necessity pursuant to ►st.ref.id="I03W3NT">&sect;704.01 Florida Statutes.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|63|10:63">
<form.text>
The way of necessity shall be over the following described property of defendant &lsqb;NAME OF DEFENDANT&rsqb; in &lsqb;name of county&rsqb;, Florida:
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|63|10:63">
<form.text>
The easement shall continue until plaintiff's property located in &lsqb;name of county&rsqb;, Florida and described as:
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para>
<form.text>
has direct access to a practicable public or private road without crossing defendant's property.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|63|10:63">
<form.text>
Defendant's refusal to permit a statutory way of necessity before the commencement of this action was not unreasonable so plaintiff is not entitled to attorney fees or costs.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|63|10:63">
<form.text>
The jury award of $&lsqb;dollar amount of jury award&rsqb; is the amount of compensation to which defendant, whose address is &lsqb;address of defendant&rsqb;, is entitled for plaintiff's use of the way of necessity and defendant &lsqb;NAME OF DEFENDANT&rsqb; shall recover from plaintiff &lsqb;NAME OF PLAINTIFF&rsqb; &lsqb;OPTIONAL:, whose address is &lsqb;address of plaintiff&rsqb; and the last four digits of Social Security number are &lsqb;last four numbers of Social Security number&rsqb;,&rsqb; the sum of $&lsqb;dollar amount of jury award&rsqb; that shall bear interest at the rate prescribed by law, until paid.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|63|10:63">
<form.text>
The way of necessity shall date from the time the amount awarded in paragraph 5 is paid by plaintiff to defendant.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|63|10:63">
<form.text>
ORDERED at &lsqb;name of city&rsqb;, Florida on &lsqb;date of judgment&rsqb;.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|63|10:63">
<form.text>
The way of necessity shall date from the time the amount awarded in paragraph 5 is paid by plaintiff to defendant.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|63|10:63">
<form.text>
ORDERED at &lsqb;name of city&rsqb;, Florida on &lsqb;date of judgment&rsqb;.

►<para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|64|10:64">
<para.text>
Accountings have two phases. The first phase is on the liability to account. This form is a determination of liability. Ordinarily, the accounting itself is conducted by a magistrate. See ►st.ref.id="I035K0J">Fla. R. Civ. P. 1.490. A finding of no liability results in the usual nonjury judgment for defendant.
</para.text>

<item.reference>
<name.block>

<designator>&lsqb;'Comment'&rsqb;</designator>

►<para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|69|10:69">
<para.text>
See ►st.ref.id="I048WNM">&sect;77.0305, Fla. Stat. This example was derived from ►<field>st.ref.id="I02UL6A"</field>Florida Rule of Civil Procedure Form 1.907<trace> </trace>(b). See ►<x>&sect;10:66 for the order to issue the writ. This form contains the method of computing the amounts to be withheld in accordance with the ►<field>sst.ref.id="I05XU9I"</field>Consumer Credit Protection Act, ►<field>st.ref.id="I05V14M"</field>Title 15 U.S.C.A. &sect;1673(b). It is based on the minimum wage effective September 1, 1997. It limits the computation of disposable earnings and the deductions of Social Security and withholding taxes. Federal cases do not permit the exclusion of other items although many forms of Florida writs do so. See ►<field>cc.ref.id="I03W4UL"</field>First Nat. Bank v. Hasty, 415 F. Supp. 170 (E.D. Mich. 1976), aff'd, 573 F.2d 1310 (6th Cir. 1977) and aff'd, 573 F.2d 1310 (6th Cir. 1977). The form in this section is not for a writ connected with child support or alimony. The form for child support or alimony is in ►<x>&sect;10:70. The form includes the exemption provided in ►<field>st.ref.id="I02XEB8"</field>section 222.11, Florida Statutes for the head of a family that most writs do not.
</x>
</para.text>
</para>
</section.body>

<form.line align="l">
  ►THE STATE OF FLORIDA:
</form.line>


<signature.block ref="manual">
  
  <signature.group position="r">
    
  </signature.group>
  
</signature.block>
<form.text>
YOU ARE COMMANDED to summon garnishee <inline.instr>&lsqb;NAME OF GARNISHEE&rsqb;</inline.instr> to serve an answer to this writ on <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of petitioner's attorney&rsqb;</inline.instr>, petitioner's attorney, whose address is <inline.instr>&lsqb;address of petitioner's attorney&rsqb;</inline.instr>, within 20 days after service of this writ, exclusive of the day of service, and to file the original with the clerk of this court either before service on the attorney or immediately thereafter, stating:
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|70|10:70">
<form.text>
whether respondent &lsqb;NAME OF RESPONDENT&rsqb; is employed by garnishee, and
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|70|10:70">
<form.text>
if so, the amount of periodic payments of salary or wages payable to respondent,
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para>
<form.text>
and requiring garnishee to withhold from each payment due or coming due of respondent's salary or wages after the service of this writ the amount exceeding:
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.item>
<name.block>
<designator>(a)</designator>
</name.block>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|70|10:70">
<form.text>
$&lsqb;dollar amount of weekly amount&rsqb; if respondent is paid weekly;
</form.text>
</form.para>
</form.item>
<form.item>
<name.block>
<designator>(b)</designator>
</name.block>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|70|10:70">
<form.text>
$&lsqb;dollar amount of bi-weekly amount&rsqb; if respondent is paid bi-weekly;
</form.text>
</form.para>
</form.item>
<form.item>
<name.block>
<designator>(c)</designator>
</name.block>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|70|10:70">
<form.text>
$&lsqb;dollar amount of semi-monthly amount&rsqb; if respondent is paid semi-monthly; or
</form.text>
</form.para>
</form.item>
<form.item>
<name.block>
<designator>(d)</designator>
</name.block>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|70|10:70">
<form.text>
$&lsqb;dollar amount of monthly amount&rsqb; if respondent is paid monthly; and
</form.text>
</form.para>
</form.item>
<form.item>
<name.block>
<designator>(e)</designator>
</name.block>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|70|10:70">
<form.text>
in addition to the above amounts withheld, garnishee may retain up to $&lsqb;dollar amount of retention&rsqb; for the first deduction and $&lsqb;dollar amount of subsequent retentions&rsqb; for each subsequent deduction for administrative expenses.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para>
<form.text>
BUT IN NO EVENT to withhold more than the following percentages of the gross salary or wages of respondent after deducting Social Security and income withholding taxes:
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item>
<name.block>
<designator>(1)</designator>
</name.block>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|70|10:70">
<form.text>
50% if respondent is supporting a wife or dependent child other than the ones for whose benefit this writ is issued;
</form.text>
</form.para>
</form.item>
<form.item>
<name.block>
<designator>(2)</designator>
</name.block>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|70|10:70">
<form.text>
60% otherwise;
</form.text>
</form.para>
</form.item>
<form.item>
<name.block>
<designator>(3)</designator>
</name.block>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|70|10:70">
<form.text>
55% if respondent is supporting a spouse or dependent child other than the ones for whose benefit this writ is issued and if the amounts due are accrued 12 weeks or more before the payment being withheld; or
</form.text>
</form.para>
</form.item>
<form.item>
<name.block>
<designator>(4)</designator>
</name.block>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|70|10:70">
<form.text>
65% otherwise and the amount due accrued 12 weeks or more before the payment from which withholding is to be made.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|70|10:70">
<form.text>
Withholding shall continue until the total amount of $&lsqb;dollar amount of judgment&rsqb; is satisfied or defendant's employment by garnishee terminates or the further order of this court. Withheld payments shall be retained by garnishee until the further order of this court, but if garnishee is deducting payments under any prior income deduction order or continuing garnishment for alimony or child support, application must be made to this court to determine the amounts to be withheld and their allocation.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|70|10:70">
<form.text>
A failure to comply with this writ may result in garnishee paying the garnished amounts twice and garnishee being held in contempt of court.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|70|10:70">
<form.text>
ORDERED at &lsqb;name of city&rsqb;, Florida on &lsqb;date of garnishment&rsqb;.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|70|10:70">
<form.text>
65% otherwise and the amount due accrued 12 weeks or more before the payment from which withholding is to be made.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|70|10:70">
<form.text>
Withholding shall continue until the total amount of $&lsqb;dollar amount of judgment&rsqb; is satisfied or defendant's employment by garnishee terminates or the further order of this court. Withheld payments shall be retained by garnishee until the further order of this court, but if garnishee is deducting payments under any prior income deduction order or continuing garnishment for alimony or child support, application must be made to this court to determine the amounts to be withheld and their allocation.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|70|10:70">
<form.text>
A failure to comply with this writ may result in garnishee paying the garnished amounts twice and garnishee being held in contempt of court.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|70|10:70">
<form.text>
ORDERED at &lsqb;name of city&rsqb;, Florida on &lsqb;date of garnishment&rsqb;.
</form.text>
</form.para>

The method of computing the exemption under the ►<field>sst.ref.id="I044SL6"</field>Consumer Credit Protection Act, ►<field>st.ref.id="I047LQ2"</field>Title 15 U.S.C.A. &sect;1673(b), is shown in ►<x>section 10:69. <section.front>
<outline.name.block>
<label>&sect;</label>
<designator>10:75</designator>
<name>Final disposition form</name>
</outline.name.block>
<online.view>
<online.view.item>Author's Comment</online.view.item>
</online.view>
</section.front>
<section.body>
►<para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|75|10:75">
<para.text>
See ►st.ref.id="I048OIS">Fla. R. Civ. P. 1.545. The Supreme Court adopted <trace>►</trace>Form 1.998 in civil procedure and <trace>►</trace>Form 12.999 in family procedure. The appropriate form must be filed by the plaintiff or petitioner in family actions and by the prevailing party in civil actions when the matter is finally disposed of. The clerk files it for a pro se party or when the action is dismissed for lack of prosecution.
</para.text>
</para>
